75.17(1): 'gag med sems la/ rnam par mi brtag cir yang spyod/ 'di nyid thob bsags 
75.18(1): che chung sbyor/ mnyam por rim par dkar nag 'od/ ma bkod sems la rnam par 
75.19(1): smin/ myong tshor bye brag 'khor lo lus la bskor/ gcig pas gcig 'gegs ma yin 
75.20(1): rang 'thad 'ong / rang bzhin stong gsal 'dzin pa smin/ mo khrims dge sdig spangs 
75.21(1): blangs pa/ tshul khrims rnam dag yul mi 'da'/ gshen rab khyim spangs rab byung
76.1(1): ba/ phyir rabs 'gro dang gshen phran shugs/ lhun grub mi gnas las grangs bsngo/
76.2(1): gdod bsag dkar nag dag pa med/ tshul 'chang bdud rtsir bsrungs las byung /
76.3(1): 'du shes mched 'phel phra rgyas dug /'gro ba'i lam ni ston par byed/ khyad par che 
76.4(1): chung sbyor dngos rjes/ lhag pa'i bsam pas rgyas 'debs byed/ gzugs med tshig 
76.5(1): smra byed brag dbye/ yid sems lus ngag yon bdag byed/ ma 'gag ltos stobs 
76.6(1): phyogs rgya che/ mthong gyur tshul khrims rnam par dag par bcang / gdug sems nyer 
76.7(1): lnga la phud pa/ sangs rgyas bder gshegs byang sems la gdug sems/ lha dang lha 
76.8(1): min la sogs drug la gdug sems/ srog lus dbang thang yo byad la gdug sems/
76.9(1): rgyan skyes bu drug la gdug sems/ gang zag spyi dang khyad par gnyis la gdug 
76.10(1): sems/ bzung yul phyi mched la gdug sems/ 'dzin sems nang mched la gdug 
76.11(1): sems/ bag chags rjes 'jug gdug sems/ 'khrul ba'i ngo bo gang shar gdug 
76.12(1): sems/ rin chen gling nor rnams la gdug sems/ kun 'byung mtshan mar 'dzin 
76.13(1): pa'i gdug sems/ 'du 'dzin las mtha' bye brag gdug sems/ 'khor ba'i sa 
76.14(1): bon gnyen sbyong gdug sems/ 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal log byed 'khrul ba'i gdug 
76.15(1): sems/ las la spyi khyab spros bsdu'i gdug sems/ gdug sems nyer lnga pa la/ zhe 
76.16(1): sdang la sogs dug lnga'i byed pa/ sbyor dngos rjes gsum dug lnga'i khams la/ gsum 
76.17(1): tshang gcig pa gnyis bye brag go /rnam smin bya byed myong ba'i rgyu mthun pa/ dmyal 
76.18(1): khams re re bskal chen gnyis/ las ma zad na de rjes bskal par nyi shu/ sras rgyud 
76.19(1): drang srong theg pa'i khongs/ 'dul ba kun 'byung dbyings dag rgyud/ gdug sems 
76.20(1): bshags brag nyob be ste sum cu gcig pa'o// //
76.21(1): 7 sras rgyud drang srong theg pa'i bon/ 'dul ba kun 'byung dbyings dag rgyud/
77.1(1): ma yengs lus ngag bsgrim par don/ 'gro drug gnas ngan kha 'khyams pas/ bskal 
77.2(1): chen grangs bgrangs thar pa dka'/ sdug bsngal rgya mtsho gting zab sbyangs/ nyon 
77.3(1): mongs 'khrul 'khor shugs drag pas/ 'gro ba bri gang mi srid ltar/ bsam 'das 
77.4(1): dpag med yod pa yin/ sngar 'das re res bsam 'das drangs kyang / bri gang 
77.5(1): med 'dra 'gro ba drangs/ gsal ba rang 'byung sems las 'byung / ma rtogs 'khrul 
77.6(1): 'khor mtha' yas pas/ rang 'byung thogs med thog can gsal/ gshen rab khyim 
77.7(1): spangs rab byung bas/ 'gro ba ma rig mun bsal phyir/ tshul khrims 'dul ba 'od 
77.8(1): gsal ba/ nyon mongs 'phel rgyas sems can mang / nyon mongs dug 'bras bsgag 
77.9(1): pa'i phyir/ tshul khrims rnam dag bsrungs thub bya/ spang bya spong byed drang srong rgyal/
77.10(1): lam ni 'gog med so sor thar/ lam bsal lam mchog 'dul ba'i lam/ thar pa 
77.11(1): chen po byang chub lam/ ma 'gag gnas shes so sor thar/ spangs bkag thar lam 
77.12(1): bde 'byed dpal/ lus kyi gos drug 'du byar gon/ rin chen rdzas lnga 'chang ba'i 
77.13(1): dbyig /tshul bcos zab rgyas 'gro 'dul bstar/ cha mnyam ma bcos lus ngag sgrib 
77.14(1): pa'i gdon/ gang phyir yul mi gtogs par byed/ yul byung yul de'i khongs su 
77.15(1): bsad/ nyon mongs 'jig rten yul 'khyal bcu gnyis/ gzung 'dzin bdag gzhan 
77.16(1): gnyis ka nyon mongs spongs// gnyis 'byung blo shar 'dzin pa'i nyon mongs spongs/
77.17(1): 'khrul ba'i blo bskyed dug rgyas nyon mongs spangs/ gting sogs bag chags 'dzin 
77.18(1): byed nyon mongs spangs/ rang ga'i 'byung blo phra rags dug rgyas nyon mongs spangs/
77.19(1): 'du 'dzin gzhi bskyed nyon mongs spangs/ rnam rtog mtha' rgod 'khrul 'khor nyon 
77.20(1): mongs spangs/ log pa snang char gsal rgod nyon mongs spangs/ bslus rjes yi 
77.21(1): rang phra ba dug rgyas nyon mongs spangs/ log spyod mi khom rang 'khor nyon mongs
78.1(1): spangs/ skye shi mi ldog rnam thar nyon mongs spangs/ gting shar g.yo 'khrug bya byed 
78.2(1): nyon mongs spangs/ nyon mongs pas ni 'dam du bying / 'dul ba rnam dag yang 
78.3(1): rtser gsal/ chu bo thur bab rgod mi 'bab/ 'dul ba rnam dag dgung mtha' gnas/
78.4(1): dus kyi rlung 'tshubs shugs kyis rgyug /'dul ba rnam dag rtsa ba'i dug mi g.yo/
78.5(1): glang chen chu zhugs phyir mi ldog /'dul ba rnam dag srung mi gol/ me lcer sbur ma 
78.6(1): chags ma red/ 'dul ba rnam dag byas la brtson/ lha yi bu mo brtag kyin sdug /
78.7(1): 'dul ba rnam dag bag thub btsun/ bdud rtsi'i zas bcud myong gin zhim/ 'dul 
78.8(1): ba rnam dag btsas legs brin/ sras rgyud drang srong theg par 'od ldan/ 'dul 
78.9(1): ba kun 'byung dbyings dag rgyud/ nyon mongs gnyen pos spangs thub nyob be ste so 
78.10(1): gnyis pa'o// //
78.11(1): 7 sras rgyud drang srong theg par 'od ldan bon/ 'dul ba kun 'byung dbyings 
78.12(1): dag rgyud/ ma yengs lus ngag stod pa non/ 'gro ba ma lus skye shi las/ sdug bsngal 
78.13(1): chen po byang chub lam/ sems nyid ye shes ma btsal gnas/ ye shes rgyal po sangs 
78.14(1): rgyas rgyu/ ye nas gnas pas ma shes rmongs/ lta ba g.yung drung rgyal po de/ ma rig 
78.15(1): byis pas slad de med/ ma shes glang chen 'dam du 'da'/ gshen rab khyim spangs 
78.16(1): rab byung bas/ sems can mtha' yas don bstan phyir/ drang srong rtsa ba dag par 
78.17(1): sdom/ yan lag mthu shor srung thub khrims/ 'dul ba phra zhib bon mchog rgyal/ dge 
78.18(1): bcu las dag 'dul bar bsrung / mi dge bcu las spangs thub spongs/ sems 
78.19(1): can las 'di rlung 'tshubs 'dra/ bag chags las sgrib ri yi grib ma bzhin/ bsam 
78.20(1): pa ma dag dri ma can/ 'dul ba bsam dag nam langs nyi shar bzhin/ shes rab 
78.21(1): bsam dag le lo bral/ lus ngag tshul khrims rab bsrungs bas/ tshad med bzhi
79.1(1): ldan g.yel ba med/ snying rje tshul khrims phyogs chad bral/ byams pa tshul khrims 
79.2(1): zhe chags bral/ btang snyoms tshul khrims le lo bral/ dga' ba tshul khrims bdag 
79.3(1): 'dzin bral/ dkar po tshul khrims dri mi 'gyur/ le lo don 'dzol bcu gsum spangs/
79.4(1): bya grub las la le los phyi shor bdud 'byung tshul khrims 'chal/ mi mthun brtson 
79.5(1): 'grus le los nag po bsam sbyor tshul khrims 'chal/ dge ba bsam log le los 
79.6(1): zhe 'gyod bcas pas tshul khrims 'chal/ don dam rtag 'dzin le los ma shes yid 
79.7(1): 'dzin tshul khrims 'chal/ 'jig rten yon tan dad log le los zhe 'dod 'gro 
79.8(1): don tshul khrims 'chal/ sdug bsngal 'khor rgyas le los 'khor ba'i bsod nams 
79.9(1): tshul khrims 'chal/ dug lnga 'khor lam le los shes rab log pas tshul khrims 
79.10(1): 'chal/ nges 'dzin gol log le los dka' thub 'du 'bral tshul khrims 'chal/
79.11(1): dngos po gshis gnas le los phyogs 'tshams gol lo tshul khrims 'chal/ rang blo 
79.12(1): rmongs sprul le los/ ji tsam dge rtsa tshul khrims 'chal/ skyabs gnas nges 'dzin 
79.13(1): le los dpal mog stag btsam tshul khrims 'chal/ rkyen 'byung rnam rtog le los 
79.14(1): phyogs 'dzin gdung bas tshul khrims 'chal/ 'dul ba ma shes le lo/ nyes 'byung 
79.15(1): cher 'phel tshul khrims 'chal/ le lo 'du 'dzin ngan song rgyu/ bdag gzhan phyogs 
79.16(1): 'dzin ngan song rgyu/ 'gro don 'go 'don ngan song rgyu/ dge bsdud ded dpon 
79.17(1): ngan song rgyu/ bya mang dge bsdud ngan song rgyu/ bsod nams rgyud spel ngan song rgyu/
79.18(1): dge spyod yul 'dzin ngan song rgyu/ dad rdzas rin chen ngan song rgyu/ dpon gsas 
79.19(1): rjes tsham ngan song rgyu/ spu shun gos bzang ngan song rgyu/ lus la rin 'gro ngan song 
79.20(1): rgyu/ nye drung gdung sems ngan song rgyu/ sras rgyud drang srong theg pa brtan/ 'dul ba 
79.21(1): kun 'byung dbyings dag rgyud/ le lo bsags 'jog ngo bstan nyob be ste so gsum

80.3(1): ma yengs lus ngag log pa spongs/ 'khrul ba'i gzhi sems log pa spangs/ blang ba 
80.4(1): yul dus log pa spongs/ sngon du 'gro dge log pa spongs/ gnang khrims 'chal ba 
80.5(1): log pa spongs/ ma nus rten rung log pa spangs/ bsad pa'i 'gags chen log pa 
80.6(1): spongs/ lha yi ma byin log pa spangs/ 'khor gsum 'khor ba log pa spangs/ 'jig 
80.7(1): rten bsod nams bcud log spangs/ me tog sbub zan log pa spangs/ seng ge'i 
80.8(1): gnas 'khyams log pa spangs/ / 'dod chags gshog rgyal log pa spangs/ rtag 
80.9(1): 'dod rdo rje log pa spangs/ g.yung drung dbyig phyug log pa spangs/ bsam gtan 
80.10(1): 'phel nor log pa spangs/ nor bu rin chen log pa spangs/ dri med bdag 'dzin 
80.11(1): log pa spangs/ skyon bral nga bden log pa spangs/ pad mo'i 'dab bral log pa 
80.12(1): spangs/ bkag pa mi mnga' log pa spangs/ gshen rab khyim spangs rab byung bas/

80.14(1): chen byang chub blo la mngon sum bstan/ sngon phyung rgyal ba de nyid mngon sum bstan/
80.15(1): ma bsgrags g.yung drung sgra 'byung mngon sum bstan/ byang sems phan 'gyed mngon 
80.16(1): sum bstan/ log pa'i smon lam 'khor bar skye ba bcu gsum dang / 'dul 'dzin 
80.17(1): gzhi dang smon lam/ bder gshegs dbang gsol thebs/ dug mtshon gzhan srog 
80.18(1): phrog smon lam/ thabs bskul nor byin thebs/ dbugs len zhe 'dod rgyu bskul 
80.19(1): smon lam/ tshong gdal rigs rjes bya ba thebs/ nor zas thabs len bon rten smon 
80.20(1): lam/ rjes 'jug bka' rten byed pa'i thebs/ gzhan la gnod bsam phra mo'i smon 
80.21(1): lam/ gnam sa phyi rgya bcad par thebs/ 'thab rtsod 'khrug chus rgyu btang smon lam/
81.1(1): zas nor rgyu btang gtong byed thebs/ bsod nams thabs spel bzang bcos smon 
81.2(1): lam/ lji bzhi thabs bslus snyed pa'i thebs/ log brgyad mtha' 'dzin skyon chen 
81.3(1): smon lam/ bka' rten gnas su 'khyams ngan yul thebs/ lung log bsngo ba rdzas 
81.4(1): song smon lam/ 'khor ba bsam grub phyis dus thebs/ phal chen rgyun gcod bsam 
81.5(1): sdug smon lam/ dka' thub bsam bya mang bdud thebs/ rten 'brel 'khor lo snang 
81.6(1): ba'i rmi lam/ shes rig mu byer bsam rtog thebs/ byang chub sems bskyed sgo gsum 
81.7(1): ma ldan smon lam/ dad gus la bsam ngan lhad thebs/ don gsum la snang ba ro 
81.8(1): chags smon lam mo/ /'jig rten bya bral ma theng 'dzin pa thebs so/ /rig pa byang 
81.9(1): sems mtha' log pas/ sdom 'chal byas pa don med song / yang dag byang sems

81.11(1): sdom 'chal byas pa don med song / so sor thar pa mdo log pas/ sdom 'chal byas

81.13(1): med song / gnang bkag bya ba rtsal log pas/ sdom 'chal byas pa don med song /
81.14(1): ngo bor ma 'grib 'dul ba gsal/ yum sras gzhung rgyud pad mar gyes/ sprul sku

82.1(1): bstan/ 'gro ba 'khrul byed tshul khrims sdom/ gser gyi gnya' shing tshul khrims lji/
